ability	<h3>ability</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>能力; 力量<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His ability is limited.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的能力有限。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She has no ability in that kind of work.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她没有做那种工作的能力。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The ability to use a language can be acquired by the act of using the language.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 运用语言的能力只能通过不断练习才能获得。</font><br>智慧, 才智; 天资<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Most schools cater for children of different abilities.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 大多数学校能够满足具有不同天资的儿童的需要。</font><br>\n
above	<h3>above</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示位置)在…正上方<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The aeroplane was flying a few feet above the sea.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 飞机正在距海面几英尺的低空飞行。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The chorus was seated above the orchestra.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 合唱队的座位高于乐队席。</font><br>(表示方向)在…的另一侧; 在…往北<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The water is smoother above the dam.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 坝的另一边水面平静些。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The greatest part of Europe is situated above the 45th degree of Northern Latitude.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 欧洲绝大部分地区位于北纬45度以北。</font><br>(表示比较)优于, 胜于; 较…更为; 高出<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Because of her beauty, she has managed to marry above her.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 由于貌美, 她得以嫁给一个地位比她高的人。</font><br>(表示环境)处在…之中; 逆着, 透过<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The captain's voice was heard above the din.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 透过一片嘈杂声听到了船长的说话声。</font><br>(表示程度)超过, 超越; 为…所不及<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You can't expect to succeed if you attempt tasks above your ability.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如果你要做能力达不到的事, 就别指望成功。</font><br>(表示等级)在…之上, 高于<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A lieutenant colonel ranks above a major.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 陆军中校比少校级别高。</font><br>(表示否定)不受…的影响; 不至于<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is above meanness and deceit.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他不至于搞卑鄙和欺骗行为。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was quite above owing his meal to the request of a little girl.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他绝不屑于应一个小姑娘的邀请去吃饭。</font><br>(表示数目)超过, 超出<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Above two hundred people attended the meeting.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 二百多人出席了会议。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>在上面<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp My room is just above.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我的房间就在楼上。</font><br>以上<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This is a military meeting for captains and above.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是一个由上尉及上尉以上军官参加的军事会议。</font><br>上述<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp As is stated above, this principle applies to all cases.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如前文所讲, 这一原则适合所有案例。</font><br>\n

beyond	<h3>beyond</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示位置)在或往…另一边; 在或往…那一边; 在或往…的更远处<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The house is beyond the bridge.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 房子在桥那边。</font><br>(表示时间)迟于, 晚于; 在…之后<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Don't stay here beyond midnight.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 别在这待过午夜。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The new law extends this ban beyond 2002.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 新法令将此项禁令延期到2002年以后。</font><br>(表示排斥)除…以外<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They had no money beyond his salary.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 除了他的薪水, 他们一无所有。</font><br>(表示范围)超出; 非…所能及<br>(表示结果)不容; 超然于…之上<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Those results were beyond dispute.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那些结果不容争辩。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His conduct has been beyond reproach.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的行为无可指责。</font><br>(表示程度)超出…的范围; 超过; 对…来说太难<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The switch on the wall was beyond the baby's reach.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 墙上的开关小孩子是够不到的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That's going beyond a joke.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那样开玩笑太过分了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It's beyond me why she married him.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我无法理解她为什么嫁给他。</font><br>(表示数目)多于, 超过<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There weren't beyond twenty people present.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 出席的人不超过20名。</font><br>(表示累加)一个接一个<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We saw peak beyond peak.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们看到山峰迭起。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>在更远处, 往更远处, 再往后<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The immediate future is clear, but it's hard to tell what lies beyond.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 近期内的情况很清楚, 但很难说以后如何。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We must look beyond for signs of change.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们应该把目光放远, 看到变化的迹象。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Snowdon and the mountains beyond were covered in snow.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 斯诺顿和远处的山到处都是白雪皑皑。</font><br>\n

color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 评判小组中包括几位知名作家。</font><br>鉴定人, 鉴赏家<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Mr. Tailor is a good judge of the fine arts.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 泰勒先生是美术鉴赏行家。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>审判; 评判; 断定<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I am not in the position to judge.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我无权作出判断。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp As far as I can judge, this book is useful.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 据我判断, 这本书有用。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was asked to judge at the art exhibition.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他被邀请当画展的评委。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They have their own minds.They will judge for themselves.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们自己有头脑, 可以自己作出判断。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It is hard to judge this case.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个案子很难断。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The court was unable to judge the case before all evidence was put before it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在全部证据被提出来之前, 法庭不能审判这个案子。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She seemed to be watching him, judging him.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她似乎在观察他, 评价他。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Who is going to judge the horses?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 谁来评判马匹的优劣呢?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Who is going to judge the long-jump competition?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 谁来当跳远比赛的裁判?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Teachers always judge their students on the final examination.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 老师常根据期末考试来评价他们的学生。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We must know how to judge people.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们必须善于识别人。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Can you judge which way to take?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你能判断应走哪一条路吗?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was calm and concentrated in judging how to defeat his opponent.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他冷静沉着, 聚精会神地判断如何打败对手。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The police judged the criminal was still in the city.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 警察断定该罪犯仍在这个城市。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The teacher judged his students had finished the exercises.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 老师估计学生们已做完了练习。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I judged, from his manner, that he was guilty.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 从他的举止态度来看, 我判断他有罪。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I judged that you had forgotten to come.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我判断你是忘记来了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I judged that it was best to resign.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我认为辞职是最好的选择。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We judge that she is the best candidate.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们认为她是最佳人选。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He's too young to judge which is better.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他太年轻, 不能判断哪一个更好。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp How will they judge which is likely to be reliable?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们如何断定哪一个是更可靠的?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Can you judge who will win?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你能断定谁会获胜吗?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Nobody can judge why he did it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 谁都无法判断他为什么干那事。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Can you judge how he finished it so soon?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你能判断他怎样如此快速地完成了这件事?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I can't judge whether he was right or wrong.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不能断定他是对还是错。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I can't judge whether he will come today.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不能断定他今天是否来这里。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I couldn't judge whether the delay was good or bad.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不能断定这样延迟是好还是坏。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I judge him a skilled worker.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我断定他是个熟练工人。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We judged the distance to be four miles.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们估计距离在4英里。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He judged them to be the best plays he had ever seen.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他认为它们是他看过的最好的话剧。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They judged her stupid.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们认为她很蠢。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I judge him to be loyal.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我认为他很忠诚。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp These horses were judged the best in the county.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这些马被评为全县最好的马。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She judged it a useless attempt to advise him.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她断定, 给他提建议是徒劳的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He judges it safer to go away than to stay.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他认为离开比留下安全。</font><br><i><font mark	<h3>mark</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>痕迹, 污点, 斑<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The spilt coffee has left a mark on the table cloth.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 洒出来的咖啡在桌布上留下了印渍。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The monument bears the mark of age.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 纪念碑上有年深日久的痕迹。</font><br>分数, 等级符号<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He walked on air for getting a high mark.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他因得了高分而洋洋得意。</font><br>记号, 标记<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Command of the mother tongue is the most distinguishing mark of the educated man or woman.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 运用本国语言的能力是受过教育的人最明显的标志。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Every garment in the shop has a price mark sewn on it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 店里每一件衣服都缝有价签。</font><br>(德国货币名称)马克<br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>在…留下痕迹, 标出<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The table marks very easily.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这张桌子很容易留下印痕。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She was careful to mark her place before she shut the book.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 合上书以前, 她小心地做了记号。</font><br>表示, 指明<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His silence marked his anger.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的沉默表明了他的愤怒。</font><br>给…打分<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He marks the score in the basketball match.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他在篮球比赛中担任记分员。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He marked the paper leniently.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他改考卷打分数很松。</font><br>\n

mass	<h3>mass</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>团, 块, 堆<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The aircraft came down in flames, and the heat fused most of the parts together into a solid mass.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 飞机冒着火坠落了, 大多数部件因高温而熔成一团。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There is a mass of stones in the yard.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 院子里堆放着一大堆石头。</font><br>大量, 大批; 众多<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I have masses of work to do.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我有大量工作要做。</font><br>群众<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The masses have boundless creative power.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 群众有无限的创造力。</font><br>质量<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This particle has very small mass.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这种粒子的质量很小。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>(使)集中; 聚集<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Troops are mass-ing on the frontier.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 部队在边境集结。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They massed well-equipped troops on the frontier.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们在边境上集结了装备精良的军队。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>许多的, 大规模的, 群众的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp These precise instruments have already gone into mass production.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这些精密仪器已经大规模投入生产。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The grand mass rally was held on the square.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 广场上举行了盛大的群众集会。</font><br>\n

险胜的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was elected chairman by a narrow margin.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他以微弱多数当选为主席。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She won the champion by a narrow margin.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她以微弱优势赢得冠军。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>(使)变窄<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The river narrows at this point.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 河在这里变窄了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The road narrows here.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 路在这儿变窄了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The gap has narrowed considerably.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 分歧大大缩小了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp In the bright sunlight she had to narrow her eyes.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在强烈阳光下她必须眯着双眼。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The doctor narrows his study.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 医生缩小了他的研究范围。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Living in the convent narrowed her views.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 修道院生活使她的视野变窄。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The benefit was narrowed.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 利益变得越来越少了。</font><br>\n
natural	<h3>natural</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>自然的, 天然的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Social problems cropped up in the wake of natural disasters.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 自然灾害之后, 出现了许多社会问题。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp In addition to natural rivers, the Chinese working people have dug many canals.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 除了天然的河流之外, 中国劳动人民还开挖了许多运河。</font><br>表现自然的, 不做作的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He spoke in quite a natural voice.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他说话声音很自然。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Try to look natural for your photograph.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 拍照时要自然一点。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Children are usually more natural in their manner than adults.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 孩子们的举止通常比成年人自然。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The movie star is always natural with other people.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那个影星对其他人总是很自然。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It is natural that he should say so.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他那样说是理所当然的。</font><br>天生的, 生来的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is a natural musician.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他是天生的音乐家。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Fighting is natural to dogs.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 狗生性爱斗。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>非常适合或肯定成功的人或事物<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is the natural for this job.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她是做这项工作的理想人选。</font><br>\n

他丢失的那辆自行车又回到他手里了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You're nearly twenty, yet you keep saying silly things like that.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你已经快20岁了, neither	<h3>neither</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>(两者)都不的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I went to see Jack and Bill yesterday, but neither one was at none	<h3>none</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>pron.</i></font><br>没有人; 一个也没有; 一点儿也没有<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Any principle is preferable to none.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 任何原则都比没原则好。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She has taken a lot of different medicines, but none has cured the disease.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她已经服过许多不同的药, 但没有一种药能治愈这种病。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp As a football player he is second to none.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 作为一名足球队员, 谁都超不过他。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There were none for him to read.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 没有人为他朗读。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp If you need a repairman, there's none better than my brother.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如果你需要一个修理工, 我兄弟再合适不过了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp None has[have] arrived yet.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 还没人来。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp None of money is mine.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这笔钱没有一点是我的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp None of guests want to stay.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 客人中没有一个想留下不走的。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>毫不, 毫无<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp After all his explanations, I remained none the wiser.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他讲了半天, 我还是糊里糊涂。</font><br>不很, 不太<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He did it none too well.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他做得一点也不好。</font><br>\n

nor	<h3>nor</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>conj.</i></font><br>也不; 也没<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Not a flower nor even a blade of grass will grow in this desert.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 没有一朵花甚至一片草会生长在这沙漠里。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He can't do it, nor can I, nor can you, nor can anybody.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他不能做, 我也不能, 你也不能, 任何人都不能。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp All that is true, nor must we forget about it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那全是真的, 我们可不能忘记。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Neither you nor he is right.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你和他都不对。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He would neither come in nor go out.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他既不进来, 也不出去。</font><br>\n
normal	<h3>normal</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>正常的, 平常的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She braced herself to lead a normal life.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她振作起来去过正常生活。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Everything is normal here.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这里一切正常。</font><br>正规的; 标准的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He received four years of normal edication at college.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他在大学受了四年正规教育。</font><br>\n
note	<h3>note</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>笔记, 摘记<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He takes[makes] notes in class.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他上课记笔记。</font><br>短信, 短笺<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She sent him a note of thanks.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她寄给他一封简短的感谢信。</font><br>注意<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I took a careful note of where I had left the bag, so as to be sure to find it on my return.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我注意记住我把提包放在什么地方, 这样我回去时就肯定能找到它。</font><br>通牒, 函件<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He presented a note to the British Government.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他向英国政府递交了一份函件。</font><br>评注, 注释<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There ought to be a note on this obsolete word.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个过时的词应有注释。</font><br>暗示, 含义<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The book ended on an optimistic note.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 该书的结尾寓意乐观。</font><br>纸币<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Here is a 5 dollars note for you.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 给你一张5美元的钞票。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>记录<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A villager had noted the number of the truck.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 一个村民记下了车牌号。</font><br>注意<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Please note my words.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请注意我的话。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Note how to do it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 注意看怎么做。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Please note that the movie starts at 7 o'clock.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请注意, 电影七点开映。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Note how he swims.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 注意看他如何游泳。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It should be noted that no one would like to take his place.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 应该注意的是, 谁也不愿代替他的位置。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They noted David to be too clever.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们注意到大卫过于聪明。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I noted a change come over his face.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我发觉他脸上的表情发生了变化。</font><br>\n
notice	<h3>notice</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>预告, 通知<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp These rules are subject to change without notice.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这些规则可不经通知就进行更改。</font><br>布告, 通告, 启示<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They announced the birth of their baby by putting a notice in the newspaper.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们在报纸上刊登启示, 宣告他们婴儿的诞生。</font><br>注意<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Nobody took notice of the mischief of the color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 别碰这门, 油漆未干。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp If workmen breathed in the fine paint spray, their lungs would be damaged.</font></i><br><font 我把颜料忘在家里了。</font><br>涂层, 漆层<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The sulphuric acid ate into the parts of the metal where the coat of paint had peeled.</font></i><br><font 那个女孩妆化得太浓了。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>画; 绘画<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The little girl paints nicely in watercolours.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is painting her a picture.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他正在为她作画。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She painted a beautiful portrait for us.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她为我们画了一幅漂亮的肖像。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The artist painted her strolling her garden.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我把门漆成鲜艳的颜色。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They have painted the table red.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们把桌子漆成红色。</font><br>涂, 搽<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Taking out her lipstick, she began to paint her lips.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她拿出口红, 开始往嘴唇上抹。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She painted herself thick and ugly.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她脸上粉搽得又厚又难看。</font><br>描绘, 描述<br><i><font him to be indecisive, negative, and selfish.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他被描绘成一个优柔寡断、消极又自私的人。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I know you dislike him, but you pair	<h3>pair</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>一副, 一条, 一把; 一双, 一对<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This pair of shoes fits me well.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这双鞋我穿很合脚。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Pairs of socks are pinned together.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 成双的袜子是别在一起的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I bought six pairs.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我买了六双。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A pair of robbers were trying to kidnap his wife.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 两个强盗正试图绑架他的妻子。</font><br>一对男女, 一对夫妇<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They will make a good pair.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他俩能结成美满的伉俪。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You are a fine pair coming as late as this!</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你俩来得这么晚, 真是一对宝货！</font><br>雌雄成对的动物<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A pair of orioles alighted on the frisking branch of a weeping willow.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 一对黄鹂飞落在拂动着的柳树枝条上。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The pair of swans nested by the river.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这对天鹅栖息在河边。</font><br>套在一起的两匹马<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This is a coach and pair.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是双驾马车。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>(使…)成对, (使…)成双<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I thought those two would pair well.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我认为那两个人将能配成很好的一对。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vi.</i></font><br>交配, 交尾<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Birds pair and build nests in spring.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 鸟在春天交配、筑窝。</font><br>\n

perfect	<h3>perfect</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>完美的, 完善的, 理想的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The shoes are a perfect fit.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这双鞋子穿着很合脚。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is a perfect wife and mother.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她是位贤妻良母。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His technique is almost perfect.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的技巧近乎完美。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The weather is perfect for a picnic.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这种天气举行野餐好极了。</font><br>完整的; 完好无损的; 无缺陷的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Practice makes perfect.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 熟能生巧。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The work is perfect in craftsmanship.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这副作品工艺完美。</font><br>完全的, 绝对的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Her husband is a perfect jellyfish.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她丈夫是个典型的优柔寡断的人。</font><br>正确的, 精确的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She speaks perfect English.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她英语说得好极了。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>使…完美; 改善<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He went to Italy to perfect his singing voice.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他去意大利提高自己的歌唱技艺。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They tried to perfect the working conditions.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们努力完善工作条件。</font><br>\n
perform	<h3>perform</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>执行; 履行<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He not only promised, but performed.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他不仅许下诺言, 而且做到了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He always performs his duties faithfully.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他一贯忠实地履行自己的职责。</font><br>表演; 扮演<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He performed well under pressure.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他在压力之下表现得很好。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The monkey performed several tricks.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 猴子耍了几招把戏。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They performed a dance for the children.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们为儿童表演了一个舞蹈。</font><br>\n
performance	<h3>performance</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>演出, 表演<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The pianist gave a fine performance.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 钢琴家演奏得很出色。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Come and see him in performance with the new band.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 来看他在新乐队中的演奏吧。</font><br>履行, 执行<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is very conscientious in the performance of his duties.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他非常认真地履行职责。</font><br>表现, 行为, 成就<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His performance in the exams was not very good.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他考得不很好。</font><br>性能, 工作情况<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Are you satisfied with the performance of your new car?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你对你新车的性能满意吗?</font><br>\n
period	<h3>period</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>(一段)时间<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Mary was restored to health after a period of medical treatment.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 经过一段时间治疗, 玛丽康复了。</font><br>时期, 时代<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This is his most difficult period.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是他最困难的时期。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He excels all other composers of his period.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他胜过同时代的所有其他作曲家。</font><br>学时, 课时<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The school day is divided into seven periods.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 学校一天有七节课。</font><br>句号, 句点<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Use a period at the end of the sentence.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在一个句子的末尾用句号。</font><br>\n

plus	<h3>plus</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示包容)外加; 另有<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Work out the full weekly rent, plus your rates.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 算出一周的房租外加房地产税。</font><br>(表示运算)加, 加上<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp What's seventeen plus nine?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 17加9等于多少?</font><br>(表示数目)在零(度)以上, 正<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp If the input voltage is plus three, it comes out as minus six.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如果输入的电压是+3伏, 那么输出的电压便是-6伏。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>加号, 正号<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He seems to have mistaken a minus for a plus.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他似乎把负号误作正号了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He calculated his gains and losses of money and the result was a plus.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他把所得与所亏钱数计算了一下, 结果是盈余。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>正的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Three is a plus quantity.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 三是一个正数。</font><br>比所示数量多的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp All the children here are 12 plus.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这里的孩子都是12岁以上的。</font><br>附加的, 称心的, 有利的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Her previous experience in social work is a plus factor.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她先前在社会工作方面的经验是一个有利因素。</font><br>\n

poor	<h3>poor</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>贫困的, 贫穷的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Many poor people gathered at the gate.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 许多穷苦人聚集在门口。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The village used to be poor.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个村庄过去很穷。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is too poor to satisfy her family's material needs.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她太穷了, 无法满足家人的物质需要。</font><br>贫乏的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The farm is a very poor one.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个农场贫瘠得很。</font><br>低劣的; 次等的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp An actor who mouths his lines is a poor actor.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 装腔作势背台词的演员不是好演员。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp My handwriting is poorer than hers.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我的字还不如她的。</font><br>(身体)衰弱的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He's still in poor health after his illness.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 病好后他的身体仍很弱。</font><br>可怜的; 不幸的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The poor old man had lost both his sons in the war.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这位不幸的老人在战争中失去了两个儿子。</font><br>\n

promise	<h3>promise</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>允诺; 答应<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I can't promise.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不能应允。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I want you to promise me.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我想让你对我做出承诺。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I promised that I would write regularly.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我答应要经常写信。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I can't give you the book; I've promised it to Susan.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不能把这本书送给你, 因为我已经答应把它送给苏珊了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She promised me to try her best to help him.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她向我保证要尽力帮助他。</font><br>有…希望; 预示<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He promises highly.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的前途远大。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A timely snow promises a good harvest.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 瑞雪兆丰年。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She promised to be a brilliant musician.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 有迹象表明她会成为有才华的音乐家。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp My father seems to promise himself his first journey abroad.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我父亲好像盼望他的第一次海外旅行。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>承诺, 诺言<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I'd like to come with you but that's not a promise, don't rely on it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我愿意和你一起去, 但这不是允诺, 别指望我一定去。</font><br>希望, 前途<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You show promise as a musician but your lack of practice is keeping you back.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你有希望成为音乐家, 但是缺乏实践会影响你的发展。</font><br>\n

pull	<h3>pull</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>拉, 扯, 拔<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The horse on the left side isn't pulling.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 左边的那匹马没有用力拉车。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Let's go over and help them pull the cart.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 咱们过去帮他们拉车。</font><br>拉过来, 拉动, 移动<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You push and I'll pull.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你推我拉。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She pulled the fence to pieces with her bare hands.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她用双手把篱笆拆了下来。</font><br>划(船)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This boat pulls four oars.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这条船是由四只桨划的。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>赢得, 招来, 吸引<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He's not popular enough to pull many votes.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他因不受爱戴而未能赢得更多选票。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He's hoping to pull the girl with his new car.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他希望用自己那辆新车吸引那个女孩子。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>拖, 拉, 拔<br>爬, 攀登<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It was a long hard pull for him to get to the top of his position.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他费了九牛二虎之力终于爬上了最高位置。</font><br>影响力, 吸引力<br>\n

push	<h3>push</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>推, 推动<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The door pushes easily.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这门一推就开。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They pushed past.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们从旁边挤了过去。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp If you push 敦促<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp One has to push the child or she will do no work at all.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这孩子要有人督促, 否则她什么也不干。</font><br><i><font quarter	<h3>quarter</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>四分之一<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Three quarters of the theatre was full.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 剧院的座位坐满了四分之三。</font><br>每小时之前或之后的一刻钟, 第十五分钟<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You will have a bad quarter of an hour of it, I assure you.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我敢保证, 你准得受一刻钟的罪。</font><br>两角五分的硬币; 四分之一元<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It'll cost you a quarter.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你得花两角五分钱。</font><br>三个月, 一个季度<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The output value in the first quarter was 10 percent over the same period of last year.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 第一季度产值比去年同期高出百分之十。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp In the first week the moon is in its first quarter, in the third week it is in its last quarter.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 第一个星期月亮处于上弦月的状态, 第三个星期月亮处于下弦月的状态。</font><br>上弦[下弦]; 月球周期的四分之一<br>方向; 地区; 城镇的一部分<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The city has a busy Chinese quarter.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个城市有个热闹的华人区。</font><br>住处; 营房<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She lives in single quarters now.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 现在她住在单人营房。</font><br>人, 团体<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This decision is seen in some quarters as a change of policy.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这项决定被一些人看成是政策的改变。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>把…四等分<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We should quarter a pineapple.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们应该把这个菠萝分成四等份。</font><br>使(士兵)驻扎, 供…住宿<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The troops were quartered in the city.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 军队驻扎在城里。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We are quartered in a beautiful villa.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们住在一栋漂亮的别墅里。</font><br>\n

暗中的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Can I have a quiet word with you?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我能私下和你谈几句吗?</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>安静下来; rain	<h3>rain</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>雨<br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>(雨)降下; (使)降落<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It's raining.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 天正在下着雨。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It will rain in the afternoon.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 午后将会下雨。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He went out though it was raining hard.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 尽管雨下得很大, 他还是出去了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It has rained over.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 雨停了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It never rains but pours.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 不雨则已, 雨则倾盆。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It rained large drops.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 雨点很大。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We'll have to cancel the cricket match, it's raining cats and dogs.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 雨下得太大了, 我们将只得取消板球比赛了。</font><br>\n

regular	<h3>regular</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>有规律的, 定期的, 定时的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He leads a regular life.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他过着有规律的生活。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He heard the regular noise of the clock.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他听到时钟有规律的滴嗒声。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You need to take regular exercise.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你要经常运动。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Saturday is my regular day for shopping.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我通常在星期六到商店买东西。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We meet on a regular basis.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们定期会面。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That sort of thing is quite occasional and not regular.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那种事十分偶然, 没有规律。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The verb “dance” is regular, but the verb “be” is not.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 动词dance的变化是规则的, 但be的变化是不规则的。</font><br>合乎原则的; 符合规定的; 正当的; 适当的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A period is the regular ending for a sentence.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 句点是一个句子符合规则的结尾。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I think your method isn't quite regular.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我认为你的方法不正当。</font><br>均匀的; 整齐的; 对称的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The chairs were placed at regular distances.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 椅子等距摆放着。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His nose is regular.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的鼻子很匀称。</font><br>正常的, 经常的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I had no regular education.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我没有受过正规教育。</font><br>连续的; 习惯性的; 固定不变的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He has no regular work.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他没有固定职业。</font><br>\n

request	<h3>request</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>要求, 请求<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The teachers were deaf to our requests.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 老师对我们的请求一点都听不进去。</font><br>所请求的事物<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You should have your request.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你会得到你所要的东西。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>请求, 要求<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Workers requested a raise in the wage.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 工人们要求提高工资。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I requested to go to the railway station to meet a friend.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我要求到火车站去接一个朋友。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He requested that they should come early.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他请求他们要早来。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It is requested that he should leave before seven o'clock.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请求他7点前离开。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They requested us to help them.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们要求我们帮助他们。</font><br>\n
require	<h3>require</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>有赖于…; 需要<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp All living beings require food.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 一切生物都需要食物。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The problem requires dealing with immediately.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个问题要马上处理。</font><br>命令, 指示<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The court required that he should pay the fine.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 法院下令他交付罚款。</font><br>要求, 规定<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The occasion requires formal dress.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这场合要求穿礼服。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He required to see my passport.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他要看我的护照。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They required that I (should) go there tonight.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们要求我今晚到那里去。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The border police required the traveler to unlock his luggage.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 边防警察要求旅客打开行李。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The teacher requires us that we must read English every morning.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 老师要求我们每天早晨读英语。</font><br>想要<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Will you require coffee?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你要咖啡吗?</font><br>\n

滚动<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Our dog loves a roll on the grass.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们的狗喜爱在草地上打滚。</font><br>轰隆声<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We heard the distant roll of the big guns.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们听到远处的隆隆的大炮声。</font><br>\n

scale	<h3>scale</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>鱼鳞, 鳞片<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Scales of skin peel off after scarlet fever.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 猩红热病愈后皮肤上的鳞屑就会脱落。</font><br>鳞状物; 障眼物<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The doctor removed the scale from his eyes.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 医生除去了他眼中的障眼物。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His explanations removed the scale from my eyes.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的解释使我看清了真相。</font><br>水垢, 水锈<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A scale of rust covered the steel plate.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 一层铁锈覆盖了钢板。</font><br>刻度, 度数<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This ruler has only one scale in centimeters.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这把尺只有厘米刻度。</font><br>比例(尺)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The scale of this map is an inch to a mile.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这张地图的比例尺是一英寸代表一英里。</font><br>规模; 程度; 范围<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He's in business on a small scale.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他做的是小本生意。</font><br>等级; 级别<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp For every year you've worked here you go up another step on the salary scale.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你在这儿每工作一年, 工资就会长一级。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His rapid ascent in the social scale was surprising.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的社会地位提高之迅速令人吃惊。</font><br>天平, 磅秤<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The butcher weighed the meat on the scales.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 肉贩用盘秤称肉。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>刮去…的鳞片[鳞状物]<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You have to scale the fish before cooking it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你在烧鱼之前得刮去鳞片。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The plaster is scaling off the wall.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 灰泥从墙上剥落。</font><br>称…的重量<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The fish scales 2 pounds.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这条鱼重两磅。</font><br>攀登, 爬<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The boys soon scaled the wall.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 男孩很快就爬上了墙头。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They are determined to spare no efforts to scale the peaks in science and technology.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们决心全力攀登科技高峰。</font><br>\n

severe	<h3>severe</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>严重的, 剧烈的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There is a severe shortage of fuel.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 燃料严重短缺。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Competition for the job is very severe.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这份工作的竞争是很激烈的。</font><br>严厉的, 严肃的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The general had a severe manner.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那位将军态度严肃。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Was his mother too severe on him?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的母亲是不是对他太严厉了?</font><br>艰难的, 严峻的, 辛苦的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This is a severe test.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是一次严峻的考验。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The pace was too severe to be kept up for long.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 跟上这步伐太难了, 无法持久。</font><br>朴素的, 纯朴的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is wearing a severe dress.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她穿着一条朴素的裙子。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That dress looks too severe on you.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那衣服穿在你身上太朴素了。</font><br>\n

shake	<h3>shake</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>摇动, 震动, 颠簸<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Give the bottle a couple of shakes before pouring the juice.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 倒果汁前先把瓶子摇动几下。</font><br>哆嗦, 发颤<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The shakes of the speaker's hands betrayed his nervousness.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 发言者双手颤抖, 可见他很紧张。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>摇动, 摇撼, (使)颤抖<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The earth shook under us.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 大地在我们脚下震动。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp In his anger he grasped the child and shook him violently.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 愤怒之下, 他抓住孩子狠命地摇。</font><br>握手<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He shook her hand warmly.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他热情地与她握手。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>使心绪不宁[烦恼, 惊吓]<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They were shaken badly by the news.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那消息令他们吃惊。</font><br>动摇; 减弱<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Nothing can shake the basis for my belief.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 什么也动摇不了我信念的基础。</font><br>\n
shall	<h3>shall</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>aux.v.</i></font><br>(有时与I和we连用, 表示一般将来时)将要, 会<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I shall go to London next month.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 下个月我将去伦敦。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We shan't know the results of the test until tomorrow.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们明天才能知道考试结果。</font><br>(尤用于与I和we连用的要求听者作决定的问句中)…好吗?要不要…?<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Shall we go to the theatre this evening?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们今晚去看戏好吗?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Let's look at that book again, shall we?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们再看一看那本书好吗?</font><br>(尤用于正式文字中表示允诺、命令或法令)〈正〉可; 必须; 必将<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Candidates shall remain in their seats until all the papers have been collected.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 试卷全部收回后考生才可离开座位。</font><br>\n
shape	<h3>shape</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>外形, 形状, 样子<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They are uniform in size and shape.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 它们的尺寸大小和形状都相同。</font><br>模糊的东西<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I made out two dim shapes in my dream.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我在梦中看到有两个模糊的影子。</font><br>〈口〉情况; 状态<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The market has been in poor shape lately.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 近来市场情况不好。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>做成某物的形状<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The children shaped the wet sand.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 孩子们把湿沙子堆成各种形状。</font><br>对(某人或某事物)有重大影响; 决定(某事物)的性质<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Can they shape public opinion?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们能左右舆论吗?</font><br>使(服装)合身<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This dress is shaped at the waist and doesn't need a belt.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这件连衣裙腰部合身，不需要腰带。</font><br>\n
sharp	<h3>sharp</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>锋利的, 尖锐的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Be careful with that sharp axe.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那把斧子很锋利, 你要当心。</font><br>急转的, 陡峭的; 突然的, 急剧的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There is a sharp bend in the road.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 路上有一个急转弯。</font><br>轮廓鲜明的; 明显的; 清晰的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Black hair is a sharp contrast to a fair skin.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 黑色的头发与白皙的皮肤形成鲜明对比。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There were sharp differences of opinion between the two.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 两者的意见存在着明显的分歧。</font><br>灵敏的, 机警的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Birds have sharp eyes and dogs have sharp noses.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 鸟有敏锐的视力, 而狗有灵敏的嗅觉。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The girl is sharp at music.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个女孩对音乐的感受力很敏锐。</font><br>辛辣的, 刺骨[鼻, 眼, 耳]的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The branch broke with a sharp crack.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 树枝折断时发出刺耳的劈啪声。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This salad dressing has a sharp taste.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这种色拉调味品味道辛辣。</font><br>蓄意中伤的; 尖刻的; 严厉的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She got a sharp reproach from her boss.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她受到了上司的严厉训斥。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I have to be sharp with him.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不得不对他严厉些。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>准时地<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Please be on hand at 12 sharp.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请在十二点整到这里来。</font><br>突然地, 急剧地<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The road turns sharp to the left.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 公路向左急转弯。</font><br>\n

significant	<h3>significant</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>重要的, 重大的, 可观的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This is a significant contribution to knowledge.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是对知识的重大贡献。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Your success today may be significant for your whole future.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你今天的成功对你的整个未来可能是重要的。</font><br>有意义的, 有用意的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I don't think that is significant.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我认为那没有什么用意。</font><br>意味深长的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He gave her a significant look.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他意味深长地看了她一眼。</font><br>\n
similar	<h3>similar</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>类似的; 同类的; 相似的; 同样的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The two boys look very similar.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这两个孩子看上去很相似。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They are similar in appearance.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们在外貌上相似。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp My problems are very similar to yours.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我的问题和你的差不多。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Similar triangles have equal angles.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 相似三角形有相等的角。</font><br>\n
simple	<h3>simple</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>简单的; 容易的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He wrote a story in simple English.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他用简单的英语写了一则故事。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The point I am making is a very simple one.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我想提出的论点很简单。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It should be quite simple; I don't envisage any difficulty.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这事应该很简单, 我想不会有什么困难。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The book is quite simple to use.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这本书使用简单。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The plan sounds simple enough but it won't be so simple to put it into action.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个计划听起来相当简单, 但是要将它付诸实施却没有那么容易。</font><br>朴素的; 简朴的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We use bricks and branches of trees to form a simple shelter.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们用砖和树枝搭成一个简陋的避难所。</font><br>自然的; 率直的; 天真的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is a simple and well liked man.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他是一个纯朴可爱的人。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was as simple as a child.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他像孩子一样天真。</font><br>易受骗的; 迟钝的, 头脑简单的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You may be joking but she's simple enough to believe you.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你也许是在开玩笑, 但她却愚蠢得信以为真。</font><br>\n
simply	<h3>simply</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>简单地; 简易地; 朴素地<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp To put it simply, the new proposals mean that the average worker will be about 10% better paid.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 简单地说, 新建议意味着一个普通工人的工资将增加10%。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They dressed neatly and simply.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们衣着整洁朴素。</font><br>仅仅; 只不过<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I have never met our new neighbours; I simply know them by sight.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我从未接触过我们的新邻居, 只见过面。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp What we need is simply money, money and money.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们所需的仅仅是钱而已。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The drink consists simply of fresh oranges.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这饮料仅含新鲜橘汁。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I don't like driving; I do it simply because I have to get to work each day.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不喜欢开车, 只是因为我每天必须开车上班。</font><br>〈非正〉实在, 简直, 非常<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp My brother's English pronunciation is simply terrible.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我兄弟的英语发音实在糟透了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It is simply ridiculous to attempt such a thing.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 试图干这种事, 简直可笑。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The meat was so tough that I simply couldn't get it down.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这肉太老了, 我简直咽不下去。</font><br>\n

stuff	<h3>stuff</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>以…填进, 塞满<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She stuffed her clothes in the wardrobe.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她把衣服塞进衣櫥。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Why should you stuff yourself?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你为什么要吃得那么多呢?</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>材料; 东西<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp What is this stuff?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是什么东西?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is not the stuff.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他不是这个材料。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We must as well buy our own stuff.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们不妨自己去买原料。</font><br>\n
style	<h3>style</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>风格, 格调; 文体<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is a very popular writer but I don't like his style.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他是个很受欢迎的作家, 但我不喜欢他的文风。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The letter is written in a formal style.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这封信是用正式文体写的。</font><br>行为方式, 作风<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Flattery is not his style.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他从不对人阿谀奉承。</font><br>种类, 类型; 流行式样; 款式<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp What style of furniture do you like?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你喜欢什么式样的家具?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They sell shoes in all styles.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们出售各种最新款式的鞋。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Her dress is out of style.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她的穿着不时髦。</font><br>风度; 格调; 气派<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He has great style.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他很有风度。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp When they got married they decided to do it in style, and gave a big party.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们结婚时决定讲究气派摆一番排场, 于是搞了一个大型婚宴。</font><br>\n
subject	<h3>subject</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>主题; 题目; 问题<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This is a book on the subject of love.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是一部以爱情为主题的书。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He squeezed 10 pages out of a small subject.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他就一个小论题硬写出10页文章来。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We didn't get to the core of the subject.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们没触及问题的核心。</font><br>话题, 考虑的问题<br>学科, 科目; 课程<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She's taking three subjects in her exams.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她参加三门课程的考试。</font><br>主语, 主词<br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>常有[常患, 常遭受]…的; 倾向于…的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is subject to fever.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他易发烧。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This area is subject to earthquakes.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 该地区常发生地震。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The plans are subject to change at short notice.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这些计划一有通知就可能马上改变。</font><br>须服从…的; 受…支配的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We are subject to our country's laws.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们必须遵守国家的法律。</font><br>受约束[管辖]的, 不独立的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This is a subject tribe.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是个受他人统治的部落。</font><br>取决于…的, 有待于…的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The plan is subject to the manager's approval.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 该计划须经经理批准。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Subject to your consent, I will try again.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你要是同意, 我再试一试。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>使服从, 征服, 制伏<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He tried to subject the whole family to his will.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他试图使全家人服从他的意愿。</font><br>\n
succeed	<h3>succeed</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vi.</i></font><br>成功<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The experiment has succeeded.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 试验已成功。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She succeeded.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她成功了。</font><br>完成<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Our plan succeed-ed.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们的计划顺利完成了。</font><br>发迹; 成就<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She's the type of person who succeeds anywhere.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她是不论到什么地方都会飞黄腾达的那种人。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>继承, 继任, 继位<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp If he has no children, who will succeed?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如果他没有孩子, 谁将继位?</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>随…之后; 继续<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His speech was succeeded by a silence.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他讲演后紧接着是一片沉默。</font><br>\n
success	<h3>success</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>成功; 成就<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Success at last!</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 终于成功了！</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I wished Jill success with her studies.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我祝吉尔在学习上成功。</font><br>成功者, 成功的事迹<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is a success as an actress.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她是一名成功的演员。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The army has had quite a few successes recently.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 最近军队打了好几次胜仗。</font><br>\n

suffer	<h3>suffer</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vi.</i></font><br>受痛苦; 受损害<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I'll make you suffer for this insolence.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我会因你无礼而使你受苦的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She suffered greatly as a child.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她童年深受苦难。</font><br>变糟, 变差<br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>忍受, 容忍<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He could not suffer criticism.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他不能忍受别人批评他。</font><br>容许, 允许<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He suffered nobody to touch his flower.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他不允许任何人碰他的花。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The prisoner was not suffered to say a word.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 该囚犯被禁止发言。</font><br>遭受, 蒙受<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He suffered the humiliation of being forced to resign.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他蒙受了被迫辞职的羞辱。</font><br>\n
suit	<h3>suit</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>一套衣服<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He changed his overalls for a suit.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他脱下工装裤, 换上了一套西服。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I'll take my swimming suit.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我将带着我的游泳衣。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The piece of cloth will cut up into three suits.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这块布可以裁成三套衣服。</font><br>诉讼案件; 法律程序<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is the plaintiff in the suit.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她是那件诉讼案中的原告。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>适合于(某人)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That song doesn't suit her voice.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那首歌不适合她的嗓子。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp These styles can be adapted to suit individual tastes.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这些式样可以加以更改, 以适合个人的喜好。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>对…方便, 使满意<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Will that time suit?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那个时间合适吗?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp All this suits my purpose very well.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这一切都很合我意。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It doesn't suit her to have her hair cut short.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她不适合剪短发。</font><br>\n
summer	<h3>summer</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>夏, 夏天, 夏季<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Summer is my favourite season.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我最喜欢夏季。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Peter died in the summer of 1702.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 彼得死于1702年夏天。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It was a hot summer.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那是一个炎热的夏季。</font><br>黄金时代, 鼎盛时期<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That was the high summer of English literature.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那是英国文学的黄金时代。</font><br>岁数<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He looked younger than his 70 summers.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他看起来不到七十岁。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I went there two summers ago.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我两年前去过那里。</font><br>\n

suppose	<h3>suppose</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>料想; 猜想; 以为<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You are only supposing this on hearsay, you have no proof.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你只是根据传闻想像而已, 并没有证据。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I suppose he will be back by eight o'clock.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我想他八点钟以前会回来。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They suppose that all rich men are wicked.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们以为凡是有钱人都很坏。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I hadn't supposed that I should get the first prize.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我没有想到会获得一等奖。</font><br><i><font 我猜想他大约50岁。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They suppose the box to contain books.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们猜想这箱子里装的是书。</font><br><i><font surprise	<h3>surprise</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>使惊奇, 使诧异<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He may surprise us all yet.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他总有一天会让我们大家惊奇。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I surprised everyone by wearing a terrible mask.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我带了一副可怕的面具, 使大家受惊了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They surprised us with a visit.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们突然来访使我们大感意外。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It surprised me to see so many people there.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在那里看到那么多人使我感到意外。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It surprised them that she was such a fine swimmer.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她游得这么好, 使他们都很惊奇。</font><br>意外发现[撞见], 出其不意获得<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We surprised the burglars opening the safe.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 窃贼在开保险箱时被我们撞上了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The police surprised the thief into confessing.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 警察出其不意地使小偷招认了。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>惊奇, 惊讶<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I'll never forget his surprise when we told him.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我永远不会忘记我们告诉他时他所表现出来的惊讶表情。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Sue was overcome by surprise when treat	<h3>treat</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>款待, 招待<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She was cooking fish as a treat.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她正在煮鱼来款待客人。</font><br>乐事, 乐趣<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp These performances are a great treat to me.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 看这些表演节目对我来说是一大乐事。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>对待, 看待<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He treated me all right.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他待我不错。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Please treat the matter seriously.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请认真对待这件事。</font><br>处理<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The water is chemically treated.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这水是经化学处理的。</font><br>探讨, 讨论, 论述<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The book treats the problems of economic development.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这本书探讨经济发展的问题。</font><br>把…看作<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They treated me as their own child.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们把我当亲生孩子看待。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He treated money as having little value.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他认为钱没有多大的价值。</font><br>治疗<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The dentist is treating my teeth.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 牙科医生给我治牙。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>请客, 款待<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I'll treat today.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 今天我请客。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He treated them to a good dinner on New Year's Day.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在新年那天, 他请他们吃了一顿好饭。</font><br>\n
treatment	<h3>treatment</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>处理; 对待, 待遇<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The mayor's treatment of the problem satisfied both sides in the dispute.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 市长对这个问题的处理使争议双方感到满意。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The water is crystal clear and drunk without any treatment.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那水很干净, 不经任何处理即可饮用。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I will not submit to such treatment.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不甘心忍受这样的待遇。</font><br>治疗; 疗法<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He's receiving treatment for cancer.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他正在接受癌症治疗。</font><br>\n
