tree	<h3>tree</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>树, 乔木<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The old trees were profiled against the pale sky.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那些老树的轮廓映衬在苍白的天空上。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There're some apples on the tree.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那棵树上有几个苹果。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There's a bird in the tree.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 树上有只鸟。</font><br>树状图, 世系图<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A family tree is a diagram with branches, showing how the members of a family are descended and related.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 家谱是说明家族成员血缘承袭关系的明细分支图。</font><br>\n
trial	<h3>trial</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>审判, 审理<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He's standing trial for thieving.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他正因涉嫌偷窃而接受审判。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The case is now under trial.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 案件正在审理中。</font><br>测试, 试验, 考验<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We shall put the machine to further trial.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们将进一步试验这部机器。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We'll make a trial of his intelligence.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们将测试他的智力。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They are doing clinical trials on a new drug.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们正在做一种新药物的临床试验。</font><br>讨厌的人[事物], 忧虑[麻烦]的原因<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The recorder next door is a great trial to us.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 隔壁邻居的那台录音机响得真是让人受不了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That child is a trial to his parents.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那小孩真让他父母伤脑筋。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The loss of relatives is among the most frequent trials in life.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 失去亲人是人生最常遇到的痛事之一。</font><br>\n
trip	<h3>trip</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>旅行, 旅游, 有目的的外出<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I'll make a bus trip to the town next week.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 下星期我将乘公共汽车进城。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He often makes a round trip to the hospital alone.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他经常一个人往返医院。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vi.</i></font><br>轻快地行走[奔跑, 跳舞]<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The child tripped lightly like a bird.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那个孩子像鸟儿一样轻快地奔跑着。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is tripping along with her little steps.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她踏着小步在轻盈地跳着舞。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>绊倒<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I tripped and fell.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我绊了一跤。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He stuck his foot out and tripped me.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他伸出脚把我绊倒。</font><br>(使)犯错误<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He tripped when trying to spell this word.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他在拼写这个词时拼错了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The clever lawyer tripped the witness.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那个聪明的律师使证人说错了话。</font><br>\n

trouble	<h3>trouble</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>困难, 忧虑, 麻烦<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The old lady told me all her troubles.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个老太太把她的烦恼都告诉了我。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He has been through much trouble.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他已渡过许多困难。</font><br>困境, 险境<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The new company did well at first, but then ran into trouble.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这家新公司最初办得还不错, 但后来就陷入困境了。</font><br>麻烦, 费事<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The trouble is that he doesn't have enough money.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 麻烦在于他缺钱。</font><br>动乱, 纠纷<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She had no hand in this trouble.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她没有参与这次纠纷。</font><br>毛病, 故障<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The car's got some sort of engine trouble again.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 车子的引擎又出了什么故障。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vi.</i></font><br>费神; 费心<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I mustn't trouble if he doesn't come tonight.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 今晚他若不来, 我就不用费心劳神了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Please don't trouble to see me off at the station.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请不用麻烦到车站送我了。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>使烦恼, 使忧虑<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I don't wish to trouble them.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不愿意去麻烦他们。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp What troubles me is that the supply of raw materials is not ensured.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 使我担忧的是原料供应没有保证。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp May I trouble you to shut the door?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 麻烦你把门关上好吗?</font><br>\n
trust	<h3>trust</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>信任, 信赖, 相信<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You've betrayed my trust.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你辜负了我的信任。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is my sole trust.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她是我惟一信赖的人。</font><br>信托, 托管<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The property is merely a trust.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这财产不过是一项委托物。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She left money to her uncle to keep in trust for her children.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她把钱留给她叔叔, 请他替她的子女保管。</font><br>照管, 关怀; 职责<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She's not yet old enough to be employed in a position of trust.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她还年轻, 不能担当重任。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I shall think it is a great trust to obey the wishes of my dead father.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我认为按照先父的愿望去做是我重大的职责。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>相信; 信任<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I don't trust.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不相信。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We have always trusted him.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们一直信任他。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I trust to hear better news from you.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我希望从你口中听到更好的消息。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I trust that I'm right.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我相信我是对的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I can't trust what you say.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不能相信你的话。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You may trust me that I'm speaking the truth.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你可以相信我在说实话。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You cannot trust him to keep his promise.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你可不能相信他会履行诺言。</font><br>\n

type	<h3>type</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>类型; 种类<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The type of skirt is all the go.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这种裙子很时髦。</font><br>典型人物; 典型, 模范, 模样<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is a fine type of the youth.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他是青年人的一个典范。</font><br>某种类型的人<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I dislike man of that type.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不喜欢那一类型的人。</font><br>铅字, 活字<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Wooden types are now used only for posters.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 木刻活字现仅用于印刷广告。</font><br>活字的宽度、字体或字号等<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The examples in that dictionary are in italic type.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那本字典的例句是用斜体字印刷的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The book is printed in large type.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 此书是用大号字体印刷的。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>打字<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I can't type as rapidly as you.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我打字打得没你那么快。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Why did you type the letter when I could have done it for you easily by computer?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我本可用计算机很方便地为你打这封信, 你何必费心用打字机呢?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Every day he typed what he composed.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他每天都用打字机把他创作的作品打下来。</font><br>\n

unit	<h3>unit</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>(工作)单位<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The family is the basic unit of society.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 家庭是构成社会的基本单位。</font><br>(计量或计数用的)单位<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The metre is a unit of length.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 米是长度单位。</font><br>(课本中的)单元<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A Reading Practice section is added to each unit in Book Two.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在第二册书里每个单元都加上了阅读练习部分。</font><br>(特定功能的)装置<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp All the units employ hollow burned-clay blocks as the basic raw material.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 所有构件都用空心陶土砖做基本原料。</font><br>\n
unless	<h3>unless</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>conj.</i></font><br>除非, 如果不<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You will fail unless you work hard.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如果你不积极工作, 就会失败。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Let's have dinner out — unless you are too tired.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 咱们出去吃饭吧——除非你太累了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Substances have no tendency to expand unless (they are) heated.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 除非受热, 物质不会有膨胀的倾向。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I will be very angry unless you have already spoken to her.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 除非你已经对她说过了, 否则我会很生气。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Don't ask me to explain unless you really don't understand.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 不要叫我解释, 除非你真的不懂。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Unless paying by credit card, please pay in cash.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如果不用信用卡付账, 就请付现金。</font><br>\n

waste	<h3>waste</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>浪费; 滥用<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We must combat extravagance and waste.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们必须反对铺张浪费。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It's a mere waste of time waiting any longer.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 再等下去纯粹是浪费时间。</font><br>废料, 废弃物<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The river was thick with industrial waste.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这条河里淤积了工业废物。</font><br>荒地<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We traveled through treeless wastes.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们穿过了没有树木的荒地。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>浪费, 徒劳<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Don't waste, save!</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 别浪费, 要节省！</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Hurry up, we're wasting time.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 快点儿, 我们别再浪费时间了。</font><br>(使)损耗, (使)消瘦<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The oil resources in some countries are rapidly wasting.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 有些国家的石油资源正被迅速地消耗掉。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The long illness had wasted the old man's strength.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 长期生病消耗了这老人的体力。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>破坏, 使荒芜<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Long dry periods wasted the land.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 长期干旱使土地荒芜了。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>废弃的; 无用的; 荒芜的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This is a waste and useless tyre.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是个废弃无用的轮胎。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The land becomes waste.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这块土地变得荒芜了。</font><br>\n
wave	<h3>wave</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>波, 波浪, 波涛<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The waves are high.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 波涛汹涌。</font><br>挥手, 招手<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He saluted his friends with a wave of the hand.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他挥手向他的朋友致意。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vi.</i></font><br>飘扬, 摇摆, 起伏<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The grass waved in the wind.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 草在风中起伏波动。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>挥动…示意, 挥手(打招呼、问候等)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He waved until they were out of sight.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他挥着手, 直到再也看不到他们。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She waved me a greeting.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她扬手跟我打招呼。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She waved her handkerchief to us.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她向我们挥动着手绢。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>挥手表示<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She waved a farewell.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她挥手告别。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We waved good-bye to her at the airport.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们在机场向她挥手告别。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She waved me quiet.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她挥手要我别出声。</font><br>\n
weak	<h3>weak</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>弱的; 易毁坏的; 无力气的; 容易被击败的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Don't stand on that chair, it's got a weak leg.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那张椅子有一条腿不牢, 不要站在上面。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She spoke in a weak voice.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她有气无力地说话。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was too weak to say a word.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他太虚弱了, 一句话也说不出来。</font><br>功能不佳的<br>无说服力的; 软弱的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That was an incredibly weak answer.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那是一个令人难以置信的缺乏说服力的回答。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The teacher's so weak that the children do what they like.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这老师太软弱了, 孩子们因此为所欲为。</font><br>淡的; 稀释的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The tea is weak.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这茶很淡。</font><br>未达高标准的; 有缺欠的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Her French is rather weak.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她的法语相当差。</font><br>\n

wear	<h3>wear</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>穿, 戴<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This suit has been in constant wear for two years.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这一套衣服已连续穿了两年。</font><br>衣服<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The shop sells children's wear.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这家商店出售童装。</font><br>磨损, 损耗<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Look at the wear on these shoes.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 看看这双鞋子磨损的样子。</font><br>使用, 用坏<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp These shoes I bought last week are already showing signs of wear.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我上周买的这双鞋已经快破了。</font><br>耐用性, 耐穿<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There's a lot of wear in these tyres.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这些轮胎经久耐用。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>穿着, 戴着; 蓄, 留; 擦<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He's wearing a new coat.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他穿着一件新外套。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She used to wear her hair long.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她过去把头发留得很长。</font><br>呈现; 显出<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He wore a smile.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他面带笑容。</font><br>磨成, 擦成; 因不断使用而造成<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His trousers had been worn into holes.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的裤子已经穿破了。</font><br>同意, 接受<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Will your father wear this idea?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你父亲会接受这个主意吗?</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>磨损, 变旧, 用坏, 穿旧<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This cloth wears well.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这种布很耐穿。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The coat is worn threadbare.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这件外衣已经穿旧了。</font><br>保持某种状态<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The house wore a neglected look.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这房子给人一种没人照料的印象。</font><br>\n

wild	<h3>wild</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>野生的, 未驯化的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They hunted wild animals for food.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们猎取野生动物为食。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Some wild flowers are growing in a corner of the garden.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 花园的一角长了一些野花。</font><br>未开化的; 野蛮的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Wild tribes still inhabit part of the Philippines.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 菲律宾部分地区仍然居住着一些原始部落。</font><br>无居民的, 荒凉的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There's a wild stretch of land behind the house.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 房子后面有一大片荒地。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp After the old gardener died, the garden grew wild.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 老园丁死后, 花园就慢慢荒芜了。</font><br>强烈的, 狂暴的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It's a wild night tonight.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是一个暴风雨之夜。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The weather has been very wild recently.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 近来天气非常恶劣。</font><br>狂热的, 发怒的, 疯狂的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She felt a wave of wild fury overcame her.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她顿时觉得怒不可遏。</font><br>对…狂热[着魔]的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was wild with excitement at the news.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他听到这个消息后激动得发狂。</font><br>\n
will	<h3>will</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>aux.v.</i></font><br>用于表示简单将来式) 将, 要, 会<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I will let you know about it as soon as we come to any conclusion.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们一得出结论, 我就会让你知道。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Will you be free tomorrow afternoon?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你明天下午有空吗?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They say that it will rain tomorrow.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们说明天将会下雨。</font><br>愿意; 准备<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I will help him if he asks me.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 只要他提出, 我愿意帮助他。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp And I will take care of you, I promise.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我保证, 我一定照顾你。</font><br>(用于请求某人做某事)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You will allow us to retire.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请允许我们告退。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Help me with this baggage, will you?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请你帮我搬这件行李好吗?</font><br>(用于表示可能, 与can类似)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That will be my brother ringing.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 按铃的可能是我哥哥。</font><br>(用于表示推测, 与must类似)大概, 可能<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The man with the umbrella will be the Prime Minister.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 拿着雨伞的那个人准是首相。</font><br>(表示总是如此) 惯于, 总是<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Oil will float on water.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 油总是浮在水面上。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Man will die.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 人总是要死的。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>用意志力驱使(某事发生)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He who wills success is halfway to it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 热切争取成功等于成功了一半。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She willed herself to bury her past.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她努力使自己忘记过去。</font><br>将(财产等)遗赠某人<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He willed that his property be divided equally among his children.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他在遗嘱中讲明将自己的财产均分给子女。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Grandfather willed my brother his car.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 祖父立下遗嘱把他的车留给了哥哥。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She willed her house to her sister.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她把房子遗赠给她妹妹。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>〈旧〉愿意, 希望, 想要<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Go where you will.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你愿意上哪儿就上哪儿。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Fate has willed it otherwise.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 命运偏不如此安排。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp God wills that man should be happy.</font></i><br><font yourself	<h3>yourself</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>pron.</i></font><br>你自己<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You must have cut yourself when shaving this morning.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你早上刮胡子时一定刮破了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Look at yourself in the mirror!</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你在镜子里照照自己吧！</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You don't seem yourself today.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你今天看上去不太舒服。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You have only got to be yourself and they will all love you.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你只要表现自然, 他们就都会爱你。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Just relax and be yourself.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你要放松自然一点。</font><br>(用以加强语气)亲自<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You yourself said so.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 是你自己这样说的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Did you do it yourself?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是你自己做的吗?</font><br>\n
youth	<h3>youth</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>青年时期, 青春(期)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They studied together in their youth.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 青少年时期他们就在一起学习。</font><br>青春, 活力, 朝气, 血气<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She kept her youth.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她青春依旧。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I am determined to give my youth to the motherland.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我决心把青春献给祖国。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He lost his youth a long time ago.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他早已失去了青春活力。</font><br>青年人<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The youth of our country have[has] lofty ideals.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我国的青年有崇高的理想。</font><br>年轻人, 青年男子<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The youth of today has greater opportunities than ever before.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 现在的年轻人比以往任何时候都有更多的机会。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Several youths and girls were standing at the street corner.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 有几个小伙子和姑娘站在街道拐角处。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Some youths were standing near the bus stop.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 一些年轻人正站在车站旁边。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He billeted in youth hotels.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他投宿于青年旅馆。</font><br>\n
